56	Your PIN number is a 3-4 digit number used to validate your identity.
58	When will my PIN number used?
60	When you log into Dwolla
61	When sending money
62	When requesting money
63	When depositing money
64	When withdrawing money
65	Anytime a action is required to validate your identity
67	Can my PIN number be letter?
69	Not at this time. Please write your pin down and keep it in a safe place. Do not share your PIN number with anyone else for any reason.
70	Can I reset my PIN or retrieve it at a later time?
71	Yes.

8	SSN Help
14	.h3_dialog {
16	font-family: arial;
18	font-size: 12px;
22	.header_dialog {
24	font-family: arial;
26	font-size: 18px;

34	.h2_dialog {
36	font-family: arial;
38	font-size: 14px;
40	font-weight: bold;
56	Why does Dwolla need my Social Security Number?
57	Using Dwolla is just like using a bank. Dwolla is a licensed US Money Transmitter. As a licensed entity Dwolla is compliant with the US Patriot Act and OFAC regulations. This information helps Dwolla provide a low cost service while ensuring our service is not used for terrorism or illegal money laundering.
58	Is my SSN safe with Dwolla?
59	Yes. Your SSN is transmitted to Dwolla's validation system utilizing a encrypted connection and stored in a secure location away from Dwolla employee's and 3rd parties.
60	Will my SSN be sold to other parties?
61	No. Your SSN is only used to validate your identity and is not sold or usable by 3rd parties.
62	What is Dwolla's privacy policy and how does it effect my personal information?
63	We value your privacy. Our privacy policy is available online at all times  here .
